 The Bengali New Year is celebrated in the middle of April

 yah baishakh maheene kaa pehla din hota he
 Poela means the first and Boishakh is the first month of the Bengali calendar
 bengali calendar hindu vaidic saura maas par aadhaarit he

 Bengali people spend most of this day worshiping and visiting relatives and friends
 is avasar par gharon main khaas pakwaan banaaye jate hai
 In Bengal, this day is worshiped for the prosperity and well being of the family
 is din kolkata ke kalighat mandir main shraddhaluon kii lambii qatari dekhi ja sakati he
 The Kali temple of Kalighat is one of the 51 Shaktipeeths

 log geet gaate hai

 Book: Chauri Chaura - Revolt and Freedom Movement Author: Subhash Chandra Kushwahaprakash: Penguin Books India Price: 225 Rupahauri Chaura's Rebellion is an unprecedented event of Indian Independence Summer which has brought revolutionary aspect of peasant revolt in second phase of Satyagraha movement and achieve Swaraj
 Exposed to the disguise of the liberation struggle in which the screws were screwed
 bhartiya rashtravaadi vimarsh main chauri chaura jaisi sthaneey ghatnaon kii ahm bhoomika par durlabh dastavej pesh kar subhash chandra kushvaha ne lok smriti or itihaas lekhan ke bich samvaad sthapit karne kii jaandaar koshish kii he
 Going beyond the debate of violence and non-violence, the book explores the socio-political roots that compelled the backward, Dalit, poor people of the British colony to take such a step
 chauri chaura vidroh ke peeche asal kaaran unheen jameendaaron kaa utpeedan tha jo mukhya taur par congress ke samarthak or aadhaar stambh hua karte the
 This book will take you to that unknown village of Chauri Chaura of 1922, which was to shape the freedom movement in the coming years
 yah kitaab academik pramanikta ke saath apane samay ke ek behtareen kathakaar kii bejod kissagoi kii jameen par viksit hui he
 chauri-chaura incident: On February 4, 1922, at 4 pm, more than two thousand villagers led by farmers surrounded the Chauri Chaura police station in Gorakhpur district of Uttar Pradesh
 british raaj ke lambey utpeedan or apmaan kii pratikriya main unhone thana bhawan main aag laga di, jisamen chupe hue 24 sipaahi jalakar mar gaye
 This incident has been mentioned in the book at some place, 'chauri Chaura police station was surrounded and set on fire
 aag dhadhakane ke baad jo sipaahi baahar bhaagane lage, unhen bheed ne peet-peet kar unki laashon ko jalte thane main phenk diya
 It was not a normal incident to blow up the Chauri Chaura police station
 1857 ke baad yah vah pehla krity tha, jisane puure british samrajya ko hilaa diya tha or isaki gunj puri duniya main sunai di thi
 News of this rebellion appeared prominently in newspapers not only in Britain, America, Australia, Soviet Union, Japan etc
 is karrwai ko anjaam dene waalon ne gandhivadi vichaardhaara or gandhi ke chamatkaaron kaa sahaara lete hue haashie ke samaaj kii golbandi to kii hi, unhone duniya main aparaajey hone kaa dambh bharne vaale british samrajya ko bhi natmastak kiya, saath hi saath gandhivaad or uske chhadam swaraj kaa pardaafash bhi kiya
 He also showed that when the back of the poor has been peeled off with a whip, rubbing salt, chilli on it and the administration is enjoying it, then the society, called untouchables, breaks the boundaries of caste and religion, takes the flag of revolution in its hands Takes
 tab use kisi padhe, likhe, chaalaak yaa dhoort netritv kii jarurat nahin hoti
 This rebellion was against both the native feudals and the foreign government, who together were sucking the blood of poor peasants
 kyon padhein yah kitaab?is pustak kii adhikansh saamagree mul british dastavejon par aadhaarit he jo desh or videshon se jutai gai he
 This book seems to be the first authentic book available in Hindi based on newly acquired documents, facts and conversations with local people related to Chauri Chaura incident
 is kitaab main chauri-chauri kii ghatana se judi aisi durlabh tasviren bhi hai jo shaayad aapako ek hi jagah par uplabdh na hon
